Obligation:
Clauses:

totient_phi(1, 1) :- !.
totient_phi(M, Phi) :- t_phi(M, Phi, 1, 0).
t_phi(M, Phi, M, Phi) :- !.
t_phi(M, Phi, K, C) :- ','(<(K, M), ','(coprime(K, M), ','(!, ','(is(C1, +(C, 1)), ','(is(K1, +(K, 1)), t_phi(M, Phi, K1, C1)))))).
t_phi(M, Phi, K, C) :- ','(<(K, M), ','(is(K1, +(K, 1)), t_phi(M, Phi, K1, C))).
coprime(X, Y) :- gcd(X, Y, 1).
gcd(X, 0, X) :- >(X, 0).
gcd(X, Y, G) :- ','(>(Y, 0), ','(is(Z, mod(X, Y)), gcd(Y, Z, G))).
